    $( "#headersearch" ).autocomplete({
        minLength: 1,
		 select: function( event, ui ) {
	  if(ui.item.flag==2 || ui.item.flag==9 || ui.item.flag==6 || ui.item.flag==5)
	  {
		window.location.href=ui.item.elem_id;
		return false;
	  }
	  $.ajax({
					type: "POST",
					data: { elem1: ui.item.label,elem2: ui.item.elem_id,elem3: ui.item.flag},
					url: "/users/busqueda_autocomp",
					success: function(msg){
						if(msg!='')
						{
							window.location.href=msg;
						}
					}
				});

      },
        source: function( request, response ) {
            var term = request.term;
            if ( term in cache ) {
                response( cache[ term ] );
                return;
            }

            lastXhr = $.getJSON( "/users/searchAjax", request, function( data, status, xhr ) {
                cache[ term ] = data; //TODO SEARCH  DATA
                if ( xhr === lastXhr ) {
                    response( data );
                }
            });
        }
    });

function inscribime_footer(e) {
    var r = trim($("#subscription_email_footer").val()),
        t = $("#subsc_comp_name").val(),
        o = ($("#subscribe_check").attr("checked"), $("#subscribe_check").attr("checked") ? 1 : 0);
    $("#subscribe_error_footer").html(""), $("#subscribe_success_footer").html("");
    var s = new RegExp(/^(("[\w-\s]+")|([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)|("[\w-\s]+")([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*))(@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$)|(@\[?((25[0-5]\.|2[0-4][0-9]\.|1[0-9]{2}\.|[0-9]{1,2}\.))((25[0-5]|2[0-4][0-9]|1[0-9]{2}|[0-9]{1,2})\.){2}(25[0-5]|2[0-4][0-9]|1[0-9]{2}|[0-9]{1,2})\]?$)/i),
        i = s.test(r);
		
    return r ? i ? (document.getElementById("subscribe_success_footer").innerHTML = "<img  src='/images/arrow_loder.gif' alt='' />", void $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        data: {
            elem1: r,
            elem2: e,
            elem3: o
        },
        url: "/companies/subscriptionfooter/",
        success: function(e) {
		
            var o = e.split("!@!@"),
                e = o[0];
            $("#subscribe_success_footer").html(""), "success" == e ? $("#subscribe_success_footer").html("<b>¡Por favor abre tu correo </b>(o carpeta de spam) <b>para confirmar tu inscripción!</b>") : "fail_1" == e ? $("#subscribe_error_footer").html(r + "  ya está inscrito" ) : "fail_2" == e && $("#subscribe_error_footer").html('Esta correo ya está suscrito a un máximo de 50 alertas de negocios, para agregar este negocio debes <a href="' + o[1] + '">cancelar tu suscripción a otros negocios</a>')
        }
    })) : ($("#subscribe_error_footer").html("El correo electrónico no es válido"), !1) : ($("#subscribe_error_footer").html("Por favor completa tu correo electrónico"), !1)
}
</script></div>
